<span class="akn-akomaNtoso"><article class="akn-act" data-contains="singleVersion" data-name="act"><section class="akn-preface" id="preface"><span class="akn-p">Under the provisions of section 156 of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1996/constitution" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1996/constitution">Constitution of the Republic of South Africa, 1996</a>, the Bergrivier municipality, enacts as follows:—</span></section><span class="akn-body"><section class="akn-section" id="sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Definitions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_1">law</span>, unless the context otherwise indicates–</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-advertising_structure">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-advertising_structure">advertising structure</span>" means any physical structure built to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_2">display</span> a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_3">sign</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement">advertisement</span>" means any representation of a word, name, letter, figure or object or an abbreviation of a word or name, or any symbol, or any light which is not intended solely for illumination or as a warning against any dangers and "advertising" has a similar meaning;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-aerial_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-aerial_sign">aerial sign</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_4">sign</span> that is displayed or performed in the air, including but not limited to balloons and blimps that can be viewed from within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_5">municipality</span>’s area of jurisdiction;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-approval">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-approval">approval</span>" means approval by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_6">municipality</span> and "approve" has a corresponding meaning;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-areas_of_control">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-areas_of_control">areas of control</span>" means those areas set out in Schedule 1 of the by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_7">law</span>; and which may be modified or amended from time to time, which amendments and modifications will be graphically depicted by way of maps as prepared by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_8">municipality</span>.</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-banner">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-banner">banner</span>" means any material upon which a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_9">sign</span> is displayed in such a manner as to be fully legible in windless conditions, attached to one or more ropes, poles or flagstaffs projecting vertically, horizontally or at an angle, or attached to buildings or special structures, but excludes banners carried as part of a procession. A flag which is not displayed on an approved flag pole shall for the purposes of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_10" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_10">law</span> be deemed to be a banner;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-billboard">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-billboard">billboard</span>" means any screen or board which stands free and is larger than 4,5m² in total area; which is supported by, or consists of, a structure used, for the purpose of posting, displaying or exhibiting a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_11" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_11">sign</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-class_2_roads">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-class_2_roads">class 2 roads</span>" means the roads which form the primary network for the urban areas as a whole and which are characterised by high volumes, restricted access and fairly high speeds;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-class_3_roads">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-class_3_roads">class 3 roads</span>" means roads that distribute traffic between the principal residential, industrial and business districts of the town and which form the link between the primary network (<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-class_2_roads" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_12" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_12">class 2 roads</span>) and the roads within residential areas;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-clear_height">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-clear_height">clear height</span>", in relation to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_13" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_13">sign</span>, means the vertical distance between the lowest edge of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_14" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_14">sign</span> and the natural level of the surrounding ground, footway or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-roadway" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_15" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_15">roadway</span> immediately below the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_16" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_16">sign</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-commercial_advertising">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-commercial_advertising">commercial advertising</span>" means any words, letters, logos, figures, symbols, pictures relating to the name of a business, trade, partnership, individual, or any information, recommendation or exhortation in respect of any particular goods manufactured or sold, or any particular services rendered or offered, or any event for commerce or entertainment, including sporting events;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-commercially_sponsored_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-commercially_sponsored_sign">commercially sponsored sign</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_17" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_17">sign</span> which advertises goods or services, but the erection of which has a secondary purpose, which is to promote or contribute to some recognised public or community goal or function;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-common_boundary_façade">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-common_boundary_façade">common boundary façade</span>" means any façade of a building which is built abutting a rear or side boundary of an erf and which façade is blank, that is, having no architectural features, which includes windows;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-composite_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-composite_sign">composite sign</span>" means a single freestanding <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertising_structure" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_18" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_18">advertising structure</span> for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_19" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_19">display</span> of more than one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_20" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_20">sign</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-consultant">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-consultant">consultant</span>" means a suitably qualified independent <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_21" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_21">person</span> or company that acts on behalf of, or as an agent of, an applicant for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_22" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_22">approval</span> of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_23" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_23">sign</span> in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_24" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_24">law</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-continuing_offence">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-continuing_offence">continuing offence</span>" means an offence in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_25" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_25">law</span>, which offence continues to exist after the expiry of the notice period referred to in a notice served in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_26" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_26">law</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-custom_made_design">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-custom_made_design">custom made design</span>" means the design of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_27" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_27">sign</span>, which features special effects such as specialist character cut outs or shapes or three dimensional presentations or moving parts or a combination thereof, and which is uniquely designed or constructed for erection in a particular location;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-development_board">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-development_board">development board</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_28" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_28">sign</span> displayed at premises upon which building operations are currently in progress and relating to any services being provided, work being done or goods being supplied in connection with such building operations, but excludes contract boards for building and civil engineering projects as required in terms of the National Building Regulations and Control Act, 1977 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/103" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/103">Act 103 of 1977</a>);</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-display">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-display">display</span>" means the display of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_29" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_29">sign</span> and includes the erection of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-billboard" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_30" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_30">billboard</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_31" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_31">sign</span> or structure intended solely or primarily for the support of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_32" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_32">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-billboard" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_33" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_33">billboard</span>, and includes the display of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_34" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_34">sign</span> of a business, trade partnership or individual connected with the contents of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_35" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_35">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_36" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_36">sign</span>, and "displayed" has a corresponding meaning;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-electronic_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-electronic_sign">electronic sign</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_37" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_37">sign</span> which has an electronically controlled, illuminated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_38" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_38">display</span> surface which allows all, or a portion, of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_39" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_39">sign</span> to be changed or illuminated in different ways;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-environmental_impact_assessment">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-environmental_impact_assessment">environmental impact assessment</span>" (EIA) means an assessment carried out to determine the impact (positive or negative) which any proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_40" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_40">sign</span> may have on the natural environment;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-estate_agency">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-estate_agency">estate agency</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_41" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_41">person</span> who markets or sells properties with or without buildings erected thereon and "estate agent" has a corresponding meaning;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-existing_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-existing_sign">existing sign</span>" means any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_42" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_42">sign</span> previously approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_43" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_43">municipality</span>;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-flat_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-flat_sign">flat sign</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_44" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_44">sign</span> which is affixed to, or painted directly onto a wall of a building but not onto or over windows or doors or architectural articulations and which at no point projects more than 250mm in front of the surface of such wall;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-freestanding_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-freestanding_sign">freestanding sign</span>" means any <span which is not attached to a building or to any structure or object not intended to be used for the primary purpose of advertising;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-gateway_route">"<span a strong sense of arrival or departure and which is consistent with city planning or development framework plans or policy, and which may be geographically depicted by way of maps or listed by the bound.</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-three_dimensional_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-three_dimensional_sign">three dimensional sign</span>" means a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_99" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_99">sign</span> containing more than 2 dimensions, including product replicas;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_impact_assessment">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_impact_assessment">traffic impact assessment</span>" (TIA) means a study carried out by a registered professional engineer with demonstrable experience in the field of traffic engineering that investigates the impact a proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_100" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_100">sign</span> may have on vehicle, pedestrian, or cyclist safety and traffic operation, which study should recommend any mitigating measures that may be required as a result of that impact;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign">traffic sign</span>" means a road traffic sign as prescribed in the National Road Traffic Act, 1996;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_signal">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_signal">traffic signal</span>" means a road traffic signal as prescribed in the National Road Traffic Act, 1996;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-transit_advertising">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-transit_advertising">transit advertising</span>" means advertising by means of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-movable_sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_101" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_101">movable sign</span> which is capable of being transported by road either on or in conjunction with a motorized vehicle, including trailers primarily used for advertising;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-transportation_terminals">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-transportation_terminals">transportation terminals</span>" means any area designated by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_102" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_102">municipality</span> as such, where the formal interchange of modes of public transport takes place by the public, including, but not limited to designated railway stations, official taxi terminals and bus terminals;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-urban_edge_line">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-urban_edge_line">urban edge line</span>" means a predetermined point to point boundary line as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_103" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_103">municipality</span>, which has as its purpose, the containment of urban development;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-verandah">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-verandah">verandah</span>" includes a cantilevered canopy and sunblind;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-window_signs">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-window_signs">window signs</span>" means signs which are temporarily or permanently painted on, or attached to the window-glass of a building;</span><span class="akn-p" data-refersTo="#term-zone">"<span class="akn-def" data-refersTo="#term-zone">zone</span>" means a land use zone as set out in the relevant zoning schemes or Town Planning Regulations as amended from time to time and applicable to any erf on which a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_104" data-eId="sec_1__hcontainer_1__term_104">sign</span> is displayed or intended to be displayed and "zoning" has a corresponding meaning.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Principles and objectives</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The object of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_1">law</span> is to regulate advertising and signage in the jurisdiction of the Bergrivier <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> in a manner that is sensitive to the environmental quality of different parts of Bergrivier <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_3">municipality</span>. It seeks to strike a balance between advertising opportunities and economic development on the one hand, and the conservation of visual-, tourist-, environmental- and heritage characteristics and traffic safety on the other hand. It further needs to ensure that advertising respects the integrity of any site on which it is displayed, and complements the character of the locality in which it is displayed; the by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1__term_4">law</span> thus aims to provide a set of regulations governing the use of land and buildings for advertising and signage and for matters incidental thereto.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_1" data-eId="chp_1"><h2>Chapter 1<br>Submission of applications, tariffs and general factors in considering <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="chp_1__term_1" data-eId="chp_1__term_1">approval</span>, amendments and conditions to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="chp_1__term_2" data-eId="chp_1__term_2">approval</span>, factors relating to specific signs, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-areas_of_control" id="chp_1__term_3" data-eId="chp_1__term_3">areas of control</span> and commercially sponsored signs</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_3" data-eId="sec_3"><h3>3. Submission of applications</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Other than those signs referred to in <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_13" href="#sec_13">section 13</a>(3) to 13(10), no person may display any advertisement or erect or use any sign for advertising purposes without the municipality’s approval in terms of this by-law and any other applicable legislation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">person</span> intending to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">display</span> a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-new_sign" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">new sign</span> or to alter or to add to an existing approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_4">sign</span> or submitting a signage plan in terms of a site development plan proposal, must apply in writing to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__term_5">municipality</span> which application must be accompanied by the following information in duplicate:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">a site plan, drawn to a scale of not less than 1:200, showing the following—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the site on which it is proposed that the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_i__term_1">sign</span> is to be erected or displayed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the position of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_ii__term_1">sign</span> and the building, if any, to which it is to be attached;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">every building and the existing signs on the site;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">existing and proposed landscaping, traffic signals and road traffic signs; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">the positions, with dimensions, of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__list_1__item_v__term_1">sign</span> in relation to the boundaries of the site and the location of the streets abutting the site, together with its existing approved zoning conditions;</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a drawing, which complies with the requirements of the National Building and Regulations Standards Act, 1977 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/103" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/103">Act 103 of 1977</a>), and is in sufficient detail to enable the municipality to consider the appearance of the sign and all relevant construction detail, including a description of the materials of which the sign is to be constructed, the colors to be used, and whether or not the sign is to be illuminated; in the latter event, the plan must indicate whether or not the sign is an electronic sign and, if so, full details must be furnished;</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The drawing referred to in subsection (2)(b) must have detailed drawings of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3__term_1">sign</span> to a scale of not less than 1:20 and a site plan indicating the position of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3__term_2">sign</span> on the site to a scale of not less than 1:50;</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">If a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">sign</span> is to be attached to or displayed on the wall or façade of a building, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__term_2">municipality</span> may require the submission of an additional drawing, drawn to a scale of not less than 1:100, showing—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an elevation of the building in color;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the details and position of the proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">sign</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the details and the position of every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-existing_sign" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">existing sign</span> on the building; alternatively the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_2">municipality</span> may require a colored print of or an artist’s photographic- or computer generated impression of the building with the details of the proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_3">sign</span> superimposed on such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-graphic" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_4">graphic</span> and drawn as nearly as is practicable to the same scale as that of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-graphic" id="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_5" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_5">graphic</span>;</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If the applicant is not the registered owner of the property on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_5__term_1">sign</span> will be erected, he or she must obtain the signature of the registered owner of the land or building on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_5__term_2">sign</span> is erected, indicating that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_3__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_5__term_3">person</span>’s knowledge of and consent to the application.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may require the submission of any or all of the following studies or assessments—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-environmental_impact_assessment" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_a__term_1">environmental impact assessment</span> (either the 1st stage thereof; being the completion of an environmental checklist or in its entirety),</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-heritage_impact_assessment" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_b__term_1">heritage impact assessment</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_impact_assessment" id="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_6__list_1__item_c__term_1">traffic impact assessment</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If a community or portion thereof or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_3__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_7__term_1">person</span> will be affected by the proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_7__term_2">sign</span>, it may require a public participation process prior to considering the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_3__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_7__term_3">approval</span>, which public participation process must comply with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_7__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_7__term_4">municipality</span>’s policy on public participation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_8__term_1">municipality</span> may require a signage master plan in respect of any development where the erection of numerous signs is proposed or the rationalisation of previously approved signs is required so as to allow it to consider a consistent design master plan prior to assessment of any individual <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_8__term_2">sign</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_9__term_1">municipality</span> must notify the applicant of any additional requirements it has within 21 working days of the date of submission of the original application and payment of the application tariff.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_10__term_1">municipality</span> must retain a copy of every document supplied to it as part of an application.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_3__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_3__subsec_11__term_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_11__term_1">municipality</span> may require written notification, by the applicant or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_3__subsec_11__term_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_11__term_2">person</span> who erects an approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_11__term_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_11__term_3">sign</span> that such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_3__subsec_11__term_4" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_11__term_4">sign</span> has been erected.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_4" data-eId="sec_4"><h3>4. Tariffs and general factors in considering <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__term_1">approval</span>, amendments, conditions to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__term_2">approval</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_1">person</span> who applies to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_2">municipality</span> for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_3">approval</span> in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_4">law</span> must, on making application, pay to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_5">municipality</span> an application tariff as determined by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_6">municipality</span> and no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_4__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1__term_7">sign</span> may be erected until such time as the application tariff has been paid in full.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In considering an application for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">display</span> of an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">advertisement</span> or the erection of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">sign</span> in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_4">law</span>, or an amendment or condition attaching or to be attached to an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_5">approval</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__term_6">municipality</span> must have regard to the following factors:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">The area of control in which the proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">sign</span> is to be erected or displayed as set out in Schedule 1; provided that if a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">sign</span> falls into more than one area of control or if a proposed site in one area of control may impact on an adjacent area of control, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">municipality</span> shall be entitled to determine the area of control pertaining to that application;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the locality or landscape and the advertising opportunities pertaining to that area of control;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the number of signs already displayed or proposed to be displayed on the erf and in the area surrounding the erf concerned;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">the findings of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_impact_assessment" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">traffic impact assessment</span>, environmental or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-heritage_impact_assessment" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2">heritage impact assessment</span> and public participation processes where applicable.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">that locality bound signs must relate to the lawful use of a property provided that no such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">sign</span> must be affixed to or placed on residential premises or portions thereof other than is permitted by or for home industries and legal temporary uses; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">that no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__term_1">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__term_2">advertisement</span> may be designed or displayed that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">will constitute a danger to any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_i__term_1">person</span> or property;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">will <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii__term_1">display</span> any material or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-graphic" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_ii__term_2">graphic</span> which, does not comply with the requirements of the Advertising Standards Authority of South Africa.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">will be detrimental to the environment or amenity of the neighborhood by reason of either its size, intensity, frequency, illumination, quality of design, material, proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-graphic" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iii__term_1">graphic</span> or locality.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">will obscure any other signs approved in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_iv__term_1">law</span> or its predecessor; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_v" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2__list_1__item_f__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">will be detrimental or otherwise negatively impact on the environment, whether artificial or natural.</span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_4__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to any conditions in Schedule 16, all new signs or advertising structures approved under this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_4__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3__term_1">law</span> and any successive by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_4__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3__term_2">law</span>, may remain on <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_4__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3__term_3">display</span> uninterrupted until such time as they do not comply with the provisions of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_4__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3__term_4">law</span> or any other applicable legislation.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_5" data-eId="sec_5"><h3>5. Factors relating to specific signs, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-areas_of_control" id="sec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__term_1">areas of control</span>, and commercially sponsored signs</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> must, in addition to the factors set out hereinabove, apply certain minimum standards to certain specific <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_2">sign</span> types and proposed localities when an application for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_3">approval</span> is made in respect thereof and will apply certain specific criteria to applications for the erection of signs by non-profit bodies. These specific standards and criteria are set out as Schedules to this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_4">law</span>. Schedule 1 to this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_5">law</span> indicates the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-areas_of_control" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_6">areas of control</span> in which certain specific <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_7">sign</span> types may be permitted, subject always to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_8">approval</span> in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_9">law</span> and furthermore subject to any additional requirement pertaining to a specific <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_10" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__term_10">sign</span> type as set out in the following Schedules:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 1: Areas of control;</span></span><span class="akn-item" signs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 4: Signs attached to walls of buildings (flat and projecting signs);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 5: Sky signs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 6: Roof signs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_g__term_1">verandah</span>, balcony, canopy, supporting columns, pillars and posts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 8: Signs on boundary walls, fences and construction sites;</span></span><span class="akn-item" balloons;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_k" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_k"><span class="akn-num">(k)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 11: Posters;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_l" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_l"><span class="akn-num">(l)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 12: Estate portable signs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_n" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_n"><span class="akn-num">(n)</span><span class="akn-p">Schedule 14: 16: Signs on municipal land or buildings;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_q" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_q"><span class="akn-num">(q)</span><span id="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_s" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_1__list_1__item_s"><span class="akn-num">(s)</span><span class="akn-p">On-site tourist attraction signs.</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-remark" data-status="editorial">[paragraph (s) inserted by section (4) of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment" class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The description of areas or routes in the said Schedule 1 should be read with the definitions as contained in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span>’s Zoning Scheme Regulations.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_5__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may grant an exemption from the terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">law</span> in respect of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_3">sign</span> types or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-areas_of_control" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__term_4">areas of control</span> set out in Schedules 10, 11 and 12 hereto having regard to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the area of control where it is proposed to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">display</span> the signs;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">nature of the event;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">duration of the erection or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">display</span> of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2">sign</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">size of the proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_d__term_1">sign</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_5__subsec_3__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">the outcome of any public participation process.</span></span></span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_2" data-eId="chp_2"><h2>Chapter 2<br>Standard conditions for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="chp_2__term_1" data-eId="chp_2__term_1">approval</span>, requirements, and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="chp_2__term_2" data-eId="chp_2__term_2">approval</span>
</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_6" data-eId="sec_6"><h3>6. Standard conditions for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__term_1">approval</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All signs and advertising structures must be properly constructed of the requisite strength and must be secure and must comply with the requirements pertaining thereto of the National Building Regulations and Standards Act, 1977 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/1977/103" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/1977/103">Act 103 of 1977</a>).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The applicant to whom <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2__term_1">approval</span> has been granted and the owner of the property or building to which it is attached shall be jointly and severally liable for the maintenance thereof and must undertake at least one inspection per year thereof with a view to satisfying themselves as to the safety thereof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Where any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3__term_1">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertising_structure" id="sec_6__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3__term_2">advertising structure</span> is vandalised or becomes torn or damaged or otherwise falls into a state of disrepair, the applicant to whom the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_6__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3__term_3">approval</span> has been granted and the owner of the fixture or property which or to which a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3__term_4">sign</span> is attached must within 7 working days of a notice in writing to do so, repair it.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All signs and their support structures must be constructed of incombustible, durable materials suited to the function, nature and permanence of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_4__term_1">sign</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All glass used in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_5__term_1">sign</span>, other than glass used in illumination, must be safety glass of at least 3mm thick.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Glass panels used in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_6__term_1">sign</span> must not exceed 0,9m² in area, each panel being securely fixed in the body of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_6__term_2">sign</span>, structure or device independently of all other panels.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_7__term_1">sign</span> and its support structure must be kept in a state of good repair.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_6__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_8__term_1">sign</span> may obstruct the opening and closing of any window or opening provided for ventilation of a building or obstruct any stairway or doorway or other means of exit from the building or prevent movement of people from one part of a roof to another.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_6__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertising_structure" id="sec_6__subsec_9__term_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_9__term_1">advertising structure</span> may be closer to overhead electrical equipment than the minimum distance as prescribed.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_7" data-eId="sec_7"><h3>7. Electrical requirements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All signs needing an electrical connection must preferably be supplied from the existing electrical supply on the erf where it is to be erected. If this is not possible, application for a metered electricity supply must be made to the relevant authority.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_2__term_1">sign</span> in connection with which electricity is used, must be provided with suitable capacitors to prevent interference with radio and television reception.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each power cable and conduit containing electrical conductors in respect of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_7__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_3__term_1">sign</span> must be so positioned and fixed so that it is safe, unseen, inaccessible and child tamper proof and animal proof.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_7__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Each interior high-voltage installation that runs unattended (such as a window <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_7__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_7__subsec_4__term_1">display</span>) and each exterior high-voltage installation must have an acceptable type of fireman’s switch in accordance with the requirements as stipulated in sections 6.7.2 and 7.5 of SANS 0142 1993 promulgated in terms of the Occupational Health and Safety Act.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_8" data-eId="sec_8"><h3>8. Illumination requirements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may approve an illuminated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_2">sign</span>, provided that the provisions of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_1__term_3">law</span> are complied with and that such illumination does not constitute a road safety hazard or cause undue light spillage.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Signs may not be illuminated if no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_2__term_1">sign</span> content is displayed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Requirement for internal illumination or electronic signs:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Internally illuminated and electronic signs may only be displayed in areas of partial and minimum control and may not exceed 2,1m² in size. This size condition may be waived, up to a maximum size of 4,5m² in any such area upon receipt of an environmental and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-heritage_impact_assessment" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">heritage impact assessment</span> showing no detrimental impact will be caused by the proposed <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_2">display</span>, or to any larger size specified by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_3">municipality</span> in an area designated by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_4">municipality</span> as a district in which illuminated or electronic signs are to be encouraged;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">electronic signs may not have subliminal flashes; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">prior to erection, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span> may require a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_impact_assessment" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2">traffic impact assessment</span>, environmental and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-heritage_impact_assessment" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_3">heritage impact assessment</span> to be conducted, the results of which must indicate that no detrimental impact on traffic is envisaged. In addition the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_4">municipality</span> may require subsequent traffic monitoring of any internally illuminated or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-electronic_sign" id="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_5" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_5">electronic sign</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_8__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Requirements for external illumination:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">the light source emanating from floodlights must not be visible to traffic travelling in either direction;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">floodlights must not be positioned so as to create any undue light spillage beyond the surface area of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">sign</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">approved way leaves must be obtained from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_8__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">municipality</span> prior to any excavations for the installation of signs. This also applies for signs to be erected in the vicinity of overhead power lines.</span></span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_9" data-eId="sec_9"><h3>9. Road traffic safety requirements</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Signs may not be erected in an area where they are an unacceptable distraction for drivers, which acceptability may be determined in terms of the guidelines laid down in the S.A. Road Traffic Signs Manual.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Electronic signs may not be permitted if they are visible from class 2 or 3 roads, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-gateway_route" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_1">gateway route</span> or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-scenic_drive" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_2">scenic drive</span> unless expressly approved in writing by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_2__term_3">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Advertising on bridges, towers, telecommunication masts, pylons or street poles shall not be permitted.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-graphic" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">graphic</span> content of signs must not have the potential to be visually interpreted as a road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__term_2">traffic sign</span>, due to any factor, including but not limited to the following:</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">any stylised or pictorial presentation of a road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_1">traffic sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_signal" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_a__term_2">traffic signal</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">any word, symbol, logo or other device used on a road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_b__term_1">traffic sign</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">use of combinations of colours specified for road traffic signs, in a manner likely to lead to confusion; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">any reflectorised paint or material.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Signs may not be erected in an area where the traffic volume, the average following headway, or accident history requires a higher degree of awareness from drivers.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Signs may not be attached to or obscure a road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign" id="sec_9__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_6__term_1">traffic sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_signal" id="sec_9__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_6__term_2">traffic signal</span> specifically provided for in the South African Road Traffic Signs Manual or the South African Development Community Road Traffic Signs Manual.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Signs may not be erected within the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-road_reserve" id="sec_9__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_7__term_1">road reserve</span> of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_road" id="sec_9__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_7__term_2">public road</span> unless expressly approved by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_7__term_3">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When located at signalized traffic intersections, signs may not have the colours red or yellow or green as main colours and may not obscure or interfere with any road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign" id="sec_9__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_8__term_1">traffic sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_signal" id="sec_9__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_8__term_2">traffic signal</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Electronic signs shall not be permitted within 80 metres of the perimeter of a signalised traffic intersection.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Flashing or running messages or variable transition messages that have a message change interval of greater than 0,3 seconds or have transition effects between message changes shall not be permitted if viewable from a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_road" id="sec_9__subsec_10__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_10__term_1">public road</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Static <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_9__subsec_11__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_11__term_1">display</span>, simple transition signs must <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_9__subsec_11__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_11__term_2">display</span> a complete frame for an information cycle length of not less than 60 seconds when visible from a signalised traffic intersection and 30 seconds at other locations.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_12" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_12"><span class="akn-num">(12)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All signs larger than 4,5m²erected adjacent to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_road" id="sec_9__subsec_12__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_12__term_1">public road</span> or in a railway reserve intended to advertise to persons using class 2 and 3 roads must be spaced a minimum specified distance from any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__subsec_12__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_12__term_2">sign</span> or road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign" id="sec_9__subsec_12__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_12__term_3">traffic sign</span>, such distance measured parallel to the center line of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-roadway" id="sec_9__subsec_12__term_4" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_12__term_4">roadway</span>, in accordance with the measurements set out in Table 1 below:</span></span></section><h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="sec_9__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1">Table 1</h3>
<h3 class="akn-crossHeading" id="sec_9__hcontainer_2" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_2">Linear spacing between signs</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_9__hcontainer_3" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><table id="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1">
<tr>
<th><span class="akn-p">Case</span></th>
<th colspan="3"><span class="akn-p">Spacing required when visible for traffic on a road with a speed</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p"> </span></td>
<th><span class="akn-p">≤ 60 km/h</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">61–80 km/h</span></th>
<th><span class="akn-p">81–120 km/h</span></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Where a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_1">sign</span> follows a road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_2">sign</span></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">120m</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">200m</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">300m</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Where a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_3">sign</span> follows a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_4">sign</span></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">250m</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">250m</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">300m</span></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><span class="akn-p">Where a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_5">sign</span> precedes a road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_3__table_1__term_6">sign</span></span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">40m</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">70m</span></td>
<td><span class="akn-p">100m</span></td>
</tr>
