</table></span></span><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_9__subsec_13" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_13"><span class="akn-num">(13)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The minimum distances specified in Table 1 above may be decreased by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_13__term_1" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_13__term_1">municipality</span> if the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_9__subsec_13__term_2" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_13__term_2">sign</span> falls within an area of minimum control, or in other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-areas_of_control" id="sec_9__subsec_13__term_3" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_13__term_3">areas of control</span> on submission of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_impact_assessment" id="sec_9__subsec_13__term_4" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_13__term_4">traffic impact assessment</span> motivating a reduction of this spacing to the satisfaction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_13__term_5" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_13__term_5">municipality</span>. The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_9__subsec_13__term_6" data-eId="sec_9__subsec_13__term_6">municipality</span> may prepare a list or map of designated areas in which the abovementioned spacing requirements shall not be applicable.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_10" data-eId="sec_10"><h3>10. Legal requirements</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_10__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_10__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All signs to be erected or displayed within the area of jurisdiction of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> must, in addition to complying with this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_2">law</span>, comply with all other applicable legislation, including any applicable Zoning Scheme Regulations or condition of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_10__hcontainer_1__term_3">approval</span> of any departure from the applicable Zoning Scheme Regulations.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_10A" data-eId="sec_10A"><h3>10A. Design and construction of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__term_1">sign</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10A__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__term_1">sign</span> -</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">must be constructed and executed and finished in a workmanlike manner and structural details should be in accordance with existing, generally accepted and tested designs, or designed by an engineer;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">may not be detrimental to or have a negative aesthetic impact on the urban design, streetscape, or the character of the surrounding area by way of design of the structure or device;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">must have great appearance and consist of durable materials in accordance with function, nature and permanence of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">advertisement</span>, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">sign</span> or structure, and materials such as cloth, canvas, cardboard, paper or synthetic cardboard should be used only when essential to the nature and function of a particular <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_c__term_3">sign</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">must have a great appearance in terms of advertisemnt content and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_d__term_1">sign</span> writing, and an untidy handwritten message should be avoided as far as possible;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">may not interfere with an electrical services provision or any other accessory;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">deface a building facade;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">must be rigidly and securely attached, supported, or anchored in a safe manner so that unwanted movement in any direction is prevented;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_h" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_h"><span class="akn-num">(h)</span><span class="akn-p">must be capable of effectively securing, supporting, and maintaining not less than twice its mass with the addition of any force to which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_h__term_1">sign</span> may be subjected, including wind pressure;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">must, wherever necessary in accordance with the nature of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_i__term_1">sign</span> and when attached to brickwork, masonry or concrete, be securely and effectively attached thereto by means of bolts securely embedded in such brickwork, masonry or concrete, or passing through the same and secured on the opposite side; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_j" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_1__list_1__item_j"><span class="akn-num">(j)</span><span class="akn-p">when attached to a conservation-worthy building, must be attached with the necessary expert advice in order to prevent damage to the building.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10A__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">An Advertiser or contractor -</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">may not use water-soluble adhesive, adhesive tape, or similar material to <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">display</span> or secure a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_2">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_3">advertisement</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">may not <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">display</span> or secure a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_3">advertisement</span> elsewhere than on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-billboard" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_4">billboard</span>, board, or any structure provided for this purpose;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">must have all exposed metalwork of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">sign</span> painted or otherwise treatd to prevent corrosion, and all timber treatd to prevent decay; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">must have measures taken to prevent the entry of water into, and the accumulation of water or moisture on or in any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">sign</span>, or any part of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2">sign</span>'s supporting framework, brackets, or other members.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10A__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">All glass used in signs, other than glass tubing used in neon and similar signs, must be safety glass at least 3 millimetres thick.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">A glass panel used in a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">sign</span> may not exceed 0,9 square metres in area and must be securely fixed in the body of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">sign</span>, structure or device, independently of all other panels.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10A__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Every illuminated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__term_1">sign</span>, and every <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__term_2">sign</span> in which electricity is used -</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">must have a power cable and conduit containing an electrical conductor which is positioned and fixed so that it is not unsightly;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">must be constructed of material which is not combustible;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">must be provided with an external switch in an accessible position whereby the electricity supply to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_c__term_1">sign</span> may be switched off; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">must be wired and constructed in accordance with, and subject to the provisions of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_4__list_1__item_d__term_1">municipality</span>'s by-laws relating to the supply of electricity.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10A__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1"><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> may, in the course of displaying or removing any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_a__term_2">sign</span>, advertisemnet structure, or device cause damage to any free, electrical standard, or service or public installation or property;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_b__term_1">sign</span>, or its brackets, on lampposts may not cover or damage any markings such as codes or symbols on the posts;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">Protective sleeves must protect the paintwork or electrical lamp posts against possible damage which may be caused by brackets securing <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertisement" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_c__term_1">advertisement</span> signs agsint such poles, and the design of these brackets and the signage must be approved by the City Electrical Engineer for each type of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_10A__subsec_5__list_1__item_c__term_2">sign</span> and lamp post to be used.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-remark" data-status="editorial">[<a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_10A" href="#sec_10A">section 10A</a> inserted by section (1) of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment">Amendment By-law, 2013</a>]</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_10B" data-eId="sec_10B"><h3>10B. Maintenance of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__term_1" data-eId="sec_10B__term_1">sign</span>
</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10B__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The maintenance of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_1">sign</span> and its structure is the responsibility of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_2">person</span> who displays the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_3">sign</span> and should such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_4">person</span> fail to maintain a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_5">sign</span> the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_6">municipality</span> shall serve notice on the owner of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_7">sign</span> to undertake such maintenance of repair work within a time specified in such notice, provided that in the event that emergency work to a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_8">sign</span> or structure is required, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_1__term_9">municipality</span> may undertake such emergency work without serving notice.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10B__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If an owner fails to comply with a notice or in the case of an emergency as contemplated in subsection (1) the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span> may carry out any maintenance or repair work and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_2">municipality</span> may claim the cost of such maintenance or repairs from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_3">person</span> who displays the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_2__term_4">sign</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_10B__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">sign</span> must-</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">where possible, be located at a height that discourages vandalism;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">be serviced, cleaned and repainted on a regular basis; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">be maintained in good repair and in a safe and proper condition according to the highest standards as regards quality of structures, posting and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_10B__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">sign</span> writing.</span></span></span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-remark" data-status="editorial">[<a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_10B" href="#sec_10B">section 10B</a> inserted by section (2) of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment">Amendment By-law, 2013</a>]</span></span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_11" data-eId="sec_11"><h3>11. Approval</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may refuse any application or grant its <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_2">approval</span> subject to conditions relating to the erection or use of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_3">sign</span> and including a condition that the owner of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_4">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-billboard" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_5">billboard</span> or the land or building on which it is erected or displayed, or both such owners or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_6">person</span> whose product or services are advertised, indemnify the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_7">municipality</span> against any consequences flowing from the erection, <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_8">display</span> or mere presence of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_11__subsec_1__term_9" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_1__term_9">sign</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, at any time, withdraw an <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">approval</span> granted in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_3">law</span> or its predecessor or amend any condition or impose a further condition in respect of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_4">approval</span>, if a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_5">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-advertising_structure" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__term_6">advertising structure</span>—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">is in a state of disrepair;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">remains unused for more than 90 consecutive days;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">becomes redundant or obsolete;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">no longer complies with any provision of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">law</span>; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">is substantially altered from the original approved application by way of either structure or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-graphic" id="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">graphic</span> content.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should an approved <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_1">sign</span> not be erected within 12 months from the date of <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_2">approval</span> or within such other time as is specified in the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_3">approval</span>, such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_4">approval</span> shall lapse, unless that period is extended in writing by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_3__term_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_3__term_5">municipality</span> prior to such lapse.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the event that the structure supporting such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_1">sign</span> is intentionally demolished before the expiry of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_2">approval</span> period, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_3">approval</span> shall lapse and no further <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_4">sign</span> or supporting structure may be erected or re-erected without the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_5">municipality</span>’s <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_11__subsec_4__term_6" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_4__term_6">approval</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All decisions by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__term_1">municipality</span> regarding applications made in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_11__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__term_2">law</span> must be in writing and will be provided to applicants within 60 calendar days of date of submission of a complete application, alternatively, if so required by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__term_3">municipality</span>, within 60 calendar days of its receipt of any additional information or assessments provided to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_5__term_4">municipality</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_11__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In notifying an applicant of its decision in terms of subsection (5), the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_11__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__term_1">municipality</span> must inform such applicant and any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_11__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_11__subsec_6__term_2">person</span> who has objected to the granting of an application of their right to appeal in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_12" href="#sec_12">section 12</a>.</span></span></section></section></section><section class="akn-chapter" id="chp_3" data-eId="chp_3"><h2>Chapter 3<br>General provisions</h2>
<section class="akn-section" id="sec_12" data-eId="sec_12"><h3>12. Appeal</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_12__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_12__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_1">person</span> whose rights are affected by a decision of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_12__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> may appeal against that decision by giving written notice of the appeal and the reasons therefor in terms of section 62 of the Local Government: Municipal Systems Act, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za/act/2000/32" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za/act/2000/32">Act 32 of 2000</a> to the municipal manager within 21 days of the date of the notification of the decision.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_13" data-eId="sec_13"><h3>13. Signs for which <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__term_1">municipality</span>’s <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_13__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__term_2">approval</span> not required</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__term_1">sign</span> not comply with the conditions relative to each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_1__term_2">sign</span> type listed below, an application in terms of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_3" href="#sec_3">section 3</a> will be required.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Subject to compliance with the conditions relative to each <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_1">sign</span> provided for in subsections (3) to (11), and any other applicable legislation, or condition imposed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_2">municipality</span>, no application for <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_3">approval</span> is required in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_13__subsec_2__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_2__term_4">law</span> in respect of the signs provided for in subsections (3) to (11).</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><i>Development Boards.</i></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Development boards must be removed forthwith when the building operations are complete or forthwith if the building operations are discontinued, or when the provisions of the services, the doing of the work, or the supply of the goods to which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_a__term_1">sign</span> relates has ceased.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span> may order the removal of any such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_2">sign</span> if the building operations have been substantially completed or discontinued or an occupancy certificate has been issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_b__term_3">municipality</span>, or the provision of the services, the doing of the work or the supply of the goods to which it relates, has for all practical purposes ceased, and such signs must thereupon be forthwith removed but no later than 5 days after the date of the order for removal thereof.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">If the premises on which building operations are in progress, are to be used wholly for residential purposes, only one <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-development_board" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_1">development board</span> may be displayed and such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-development_board" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_c__term_2">development board</span> may not exceed 3m² in total area.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">If the premises are not to be used wholly for residential purposes, no more than two development boards may be displayed and the aggregate area of both development boards may not exceed 5m² in total area;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">If the signage, whether on freestanding boards, or flexible building covering material, include any other form of third party advertising, such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_1">sign</span> must then comply with the provisions of Schedule 8 hereto and municipal <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_2">approval</span> for the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_3">display</span> thereof must first be obtained in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_3__list_1__item_e__term_4">law</span>.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><i>To Let/For Sale Signs.</i></span><span class="akn-p">These include any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_4__term_1">sign</span> not exceeding 400mm × 500mm in total area displayed at existing premises or at properties upon which a new building is being erected and relating to accommodation being offered to rent or purchase in the building, on condition that any such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_4__term_2">sign</span> must be removed within 60 days after the date upon which the accommodation to which it relates is capable of occupation.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><i>On Premises Business Signs.</i></span><span class="akn-p">These include any unilluminated <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_5__term_1">sign</span> not projecting over a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_road" id="sec_13__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_5__term_2">public road</span> and not exceeding 0,2m² in total area notifying only the types of trade, business, industry or profession lawfully conducted by any occupant or permanent resident of the premises to which it is attached, the name of such occupant, the type of activity, the address and telephone number of such premises and the hours of attendance (if any); provided that only one such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_5__term_3">sign</span> per occupant may be displayed.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><i>Window Signs.</i></span><span class="akn-p">These include any locality bound signs which are temporarily or permanently painted on or attached to the window glass of a building used for commercial, office, industrial or entertainment purposes, or any other temporary or permanent <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_6__term_1">sign</span> which is displayed within 2 metres of any window or external opening through which it can be seen from the outside such a building, on condition that no window <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_6__term_2">sign</span> may exceed 4,5m² in an area of maximum control.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><i>Signs incorporated in the face of a building.</i></span><span class="akn-p">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_7__term_1">sign</span> forming an integral part of the fabric of a building (but excluding a painted <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_7__term_2">sign</span> or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_7__term_3">sign</span> affixed in any manner onto the building), on condition that no such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_7__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_7__term_4">sign</span> may exceed 0,2m² in total area.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><i>Signs on Sports Fields.</i></span><span class="akn-p">Except when visible from scenic drives, any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__term_1">sign</span> erected around the perimeter of a sports field, to a maximum size of 2 × 1 meter each, provided further that larger signs which face inwards onto the field and are not visible from any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_place" id="sec_13__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_8__term_2">public place</span>, may also be permitted.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_9" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9"><span class="akn-num">(9)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><i>Security Signs.</i></span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-security_sign" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__term_1">security sign</span> not projecting over a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_road" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__term_2">public road</span> and not exceeding 0,2m² in total area indicating either that a security watch scheme is in operation or that a security company has been contracted to protect the premises on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__term_3">sign</span> is displayed, on condition that—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">only one such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__term_1">sign</span> is displayed on any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-public_road" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_a__term_2">public road</span> or each street frontage of such premises; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the said <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_b__term_1">sign</span> displays only the name, logo, address and telephone number of a security company contracted to protect the premises on which the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_9__list_1__item_b__term_2">sign</span> is displayed.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_10" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10"><span class="akn-num">(10)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction"><i>Sponsored, commercially sponsored and Non-Profit Body Signs: less than 4,5m².</i></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">Any such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_1">sign</span> whether erected by or in connection with a non profit body or not; not exceeding 4,5m² in total area on condition that no more than 5% of the total surface area of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_2">sign</span> is used for third party advertising; and the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_3">sign</span> is not illuminated, and furthermore provided that only one such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_a__term_4">sign</span> may be permitted per erf.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">Signs which comply with provisions of subsection (a) may, when erected on municipal land, only be erected once agreement has been concluded with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>, wherein the extent of the community or public benefit as jointly agreed between the municipal department responsible for the premises or land has been agreed and the terms of the erection of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_2">sign</span> agreed, and a copy of the agreement lodged with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_b__term_3">municipality</span>.</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_10__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">All other sponsored signs are dealt with in Schedules 16 and 17.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_13__subsec_11" data-eId="sec_13__subsec_11"><span class="akn-num">(11)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p"><i>Advertising on Vehicles</i></span><span class="akn-p">Signs painted or affixed directly onto the body of a motorised vehicle.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_14" data-eId="sec_14"><h3>14. Disfigurement</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_1">person</span> may destroy, harm, damage or disfigure or deface the front or frontage of any street, road <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-traffic_sign" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_2">traffic sign</span>, wall, fence, land, rock, tree or other natural feature, or the front or frontage or roof of any building or structure in any manner whatsoever during construction or through the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-display" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_3">display</span> or use of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_4">sign</span> or the writing or painting of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_5">sign</span>, symbol, letters or numerals. Furthermore, no <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_6">person</span> may disfigure any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_7">sign</span> legally displayed in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_14__hcontainer_1__term_8">law</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_15" data-eId="sec_15"><h3>15. Damage to municipal property</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_15__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_15__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">No <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_1">person</span> may, in the course of erecting or removing any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_2">sign</span>, or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-banner" id="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_3">banner</span>, cause damage to any tree, electric standard or service or other municipal installation or property and <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-street_furniture" id="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_15__hcontainer_1__term_4">street furniture</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_16" data-eId="sec_16"><h3>16. Entry and inspections</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_1">municipality</span> shall be entitled, through its duly authorized officers, and with prior written notification to the owner or occupant of a property, to enter into and upon any premises, at a reasonable time for the purpose of carrying out any inspection necessary for the proper administration and enforcement of the provisions of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_16__hcontainer_1__term_2">law</span>.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_17" data-eId="sec_17"><h3>17. Offences and penalties</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">person</span> who—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">contravenes or fails to comply with any provision of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">law</span> or any of the standards and requirements contained in Schedules 2 to 17 of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">law</span>—</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">contravenes or fails to comply with any requirement set out in a notice served on him in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">law</span>;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">contravenes or fails to comply with any condition imposed in terms of this By- Law;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">knowingly makes a false statement in respect of any application in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__term_1">law</span>, commits an offence and on conviction shall be liable to—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">a fine or imprisonment, or either such fine or imprisonment or to both such fine and such imprisonment and,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">in the case of a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-continuing_offence" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii__term_1">continuing offence</span>, to an additional fine or an additional period of imprisonment or to such additional imprisonment without the option of a fine or to both such additional fine and imprisonment for each day on which such offence is continued and,</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">a further amount equal to any costs and expenses found by the court to have been incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii__term_1" data-eId="sec_17__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii__term_1">municipality</span> as result of such contravention or failure.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_18" data-eId="sec_18"><h3>18. Presumptions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_1">person</span> charged with an offence in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__term_2">law</span> who is—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">alone or jointly with any other <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> responsible for organising, or in control of any meeting, function or event, to which a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_2">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-poster" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_3">poster</span> relates, shall be deemed, until the contrary is proved, to have knowingly displayed every unlawful <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_4" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_4">sign</span> or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-poster" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_5" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_a__term_5">poster</span> displayed in connection with such meeting, function or event or to have caused or allowed it to be so displayed;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span> whose name appears on an unlawful <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_2">sign</span> or whose product or services are advertised on such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_3">sign</span>, shall be deemed, until the contrary is proved, to have displayed such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_4" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_b__term_4">sign</span>, or to have caused or allowed it to be displayed unless the contrary is proved;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">the owner of any land or building on which any unlawful <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_1">sign</span> was or is displayed, shall be deemed, until the contrary is proved, to have knowingly displayed such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2" data-eId="sec_18__hcontainer_1__list_1__item_c__term_2">sign</span>, or caused or allowed it to be displayed.</span></span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_19" data-eId="sec_19"><h3>19. Enforcement and removal of signs</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">If any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_1">sign</span> displayed is in contravention of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_2">law</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> may serve a notice on the owner or lessee of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_4">sign</span>, or the land owner on whose land the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_5" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_5">sign</span> is erected or displayed, or <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_6" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_6">person</span> whose product or services are advertised, calling upon such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_7" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_7">person</span> to remove such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_1__term_8" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_1__term_8">sign</span> or carry out such alteration thereto or do such work as may be specified in such request or notice, within a time frame specified therein.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A notice served in terms of subsection (1) may be withdrawn or varied by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_2__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2__term_1">municipality</span>, by agreement with the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_2__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_2__term_2">person</span> so served, or failing such agreement, by the service of a further notice.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Should the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_1">municipality</span>’s directives, as set out in the notice, not be carried out within the time period specified therein, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_2">municipality</span> may, without further notice to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_3">person</span> upon whom the notice was served, remove or alter the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_3__term_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_3__term_4">sign</span> or do such work as may be specified in such notice.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any costs incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_4__term_1">municipality</span> in removing signs, or in doing alterations or other works required in terms of a notice, may be recovered from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_4__term_2">person</span> on whom the notice was served.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_5" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5"><span class="akn-num">(5)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding any other clause in this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_19__subsec_5__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__term_1">law</span>, if a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_5__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__term_2">sign</span> is, or is reasonably considered to be a danger to life or property, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_5__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__term_3">municipality</span> itself may, without prior notice and without a court order carry out or arrange for the removal of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_5__term_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_5__term_4">sign</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_6" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_6"><span class="akn-num">(6)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any costs incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_6__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_6__term_1">municipality</span> in carrying out or arranging for the removal of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_6__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_6__term_2">sign</span> may be recovered from the owner or lessee of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_6__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_6__term_3">sign</span>, or the landowner on whose land the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_6__term_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_6__term_4">sign</span> was erected, or the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_19__subsec_6__term_5" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_6__term_5">person</span> whose product or services were advertised, jointly and severally.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_7" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_7"><span class="akn-num">(7)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Unlawful signs removed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_7__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_7__term_1">municipality</span> may be reclaimed from the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_7__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_7__term_2">municipality</span> on payment in full to it of any costs incurred by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_7__term_3" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_7__term_3">municipality</span> in the removal of the said <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_7__term_4" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_7__term_4">sign</span>, as well as payment of the costs of any tariffs incurred in the storage of such <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-sign" id="sec_19__subsec_7__term_5" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_7__term_5">sign</span> within two months.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_19__subsec_8" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_8"><span class="akn-num">(8)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Any unlawful signs removed by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_8__term_1" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_8__term_1">municipality</span> and not reclaimed within two months of the date of removal may be disposed of by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_19__subsec_8__term_2" data-eId="sec_19__subsec_8__term_2">municipality</span> to defray its removal or storage costs.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_20" data-eId="sec_20"><h3>20. Service of notices</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A notice issued by the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_2">law</span> is deemed to be duly issued if an official of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_20__subsec_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_1__term_3">municipality</span> signed it.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">Any notice or other document that is served on a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__term_1">person</span> in terms of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__term_2">law</span> is regarded as having been duly served—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been delivered to that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> personally;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been left at that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">person</span>’s place of residence or business in the Republic with a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_2">person</span> apparently over the age of 16 years;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been posted by registered or certified mail to that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_c__term_1">person</span>’s known residential or business address in the Republic, and an acknowledgment of the posting thereof from the postal service is obtained;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_d" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_d"><span class="akn-num">(d)</span><span class="akn-p">if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_1">person</span>’s address in the Republic is unknown, when it has been served on that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_d__term_2">person</span>’s agent or representative in the Republic in the manner provided by paragraphs (a), (b) or (c);</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_e" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-p">if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_e__term_1">person</span>’s address and agent or representative in the Republic is unknown, when it has been posted in a conspicuous place on the land or business premises to which it relates;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_f" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_f"><span class="akn-num">(f)</span><span class="akn-p">in the event of a body corporate, when it has been delivered at the registered office of the business premises of the body corporate; or</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_g" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_g"><span class="akn-num">(g)</span><span class="akn-p">when it has been delivered, at the request of that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_2__list_1__item_g__term_1">person</span>, to his or her e-mail address.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Service of a copy is deemed to be service of the original.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_20__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">When any notice or other document is served on the owner, occupier, or holder of any property, or right in any property, it is sufficient if that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_4__term_1">person</span> is described in the notice or other document as the owner, occupier, or holder of the property or right in question, and it is not necessary to name that <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_20__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_20__subsec_4__term_2">person</span>.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_21" data-eId="sec_21"><h3>21. Liaison forums in community</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__term_1">municipality</span> may establish liaison forums in a community for the purposes of encouraging a local community to participate in the implementation, development and enforcement of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_21__subsec_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_1__term_2">law</span>.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The forums contemplated in sub-section (1) may consist of—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">a member or members of an interest group or an affected <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_a__term_1">person</span> or community;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">a designated official or officials of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_b__term_1">municipality</span>; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_c" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_2__list_1__item_c"><span class="akn-num">(c)</span><span class="akn-p">a councillor from the relevant council committee.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-blockList" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">The <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__term_1">municipality</span> may, in the implementation and enforcement of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__term_2">law</span>,—</span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_a"><span class="akn-num">(a)</span><span class="akn-p">request the input of a forum;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_b" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_3__list_1__item_b"><span class="akn-num">(b)</span><span class="akn-p">employ any skills or capacity that may exist in such a forum.</span></span></span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="sec_21__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A forum, or a <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_21__subsec_4__term_1" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_4__term_1">person</span> or persons contemplated in sub-section (2), may, on own initiative, submit an input to the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_21__subsec_4__term_2" data-eId="sec_21__subsec_4__term_2">municipality</span> for consideration.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_22" data-eId="sec_22"><h3>22. Magistrate’s court jurisdiction</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding anything to the contrary contained in any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_1">law</span> relating to Magistrates’ Courts, a Magistrate shall have jurisdiction, on the application of the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span>, to make an order for the enforcement of any of the provisions of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_3">law</span> or of any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-approval" id="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_22__hcontainer_1__term_4">approval</span>, refusal or condition granted or applicable in terms hereof.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_23" data-eId="sec_23"><h3>23. Exemptions</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="sec_23__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_23__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Notwithstanding the provisions of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_1" data-eId="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_1">law</span>, the <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-municipality" id="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_2" data-eId="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_2">municipality</span> may, on written application, exempt any <span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-person" id="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_3" data-eId="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_3">person</span> or class of persons from any or all of the requirements of this by-<span class="akn-term" data-refersTo="#term-law" id="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_4" data-eId="sec_23__hcontainer_1__term_4">law</span> and in considering such exemption it may impose any conditions or requirements it deems appropriate.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="sec_24" data-eId="sec_24"><h3>24. Repeal of by-laws</h3>
