municipal property:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">the municipality must evaluate the proposal;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the municipality as landowner reserves the right not to proceed with any proposal prior to final approval thereof; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_d__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">if accepted, a written agreement between the municipality, the person responsible for the erection of the sign and the non-profit body must be entered into.</span></span></span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e"><span class="akn-num">(e)</span><span class="akn-blockList" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1"><span class="akn-listIntroduction">In addition the following conditions will apply:</span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_i"><span class="akn-num">(i)</span><span class="akn-p">signs with a political content will not be permitted;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_ii"><span class="akn-num">(ii)</span><span class="akn-p">the maximum size of any such sign is 6m × 3m; provided in the event of a V-shaped sign being proposed, its maximum size will not exceed two panels of 6m × 3m each;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iii"><span class="akn-num">(iii)</span><span class="akn-p">applications for billboards to be erected in terms of this section must comply with the requirements as set out in Schedule 2;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_iv"><span class="akn-num">(iv)</span><span class="akn-p">no sign erected in terms of this clause may be located within 5 metres of a property’s boundary line;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_v" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_v"><span class="akn-num">(v)</span><span class="akn-p">the name of the non-profit body must be displayed on the sign with a maximum 300mm lettering height;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_vi" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_vi"><span class="akn-num">(vi)</span><span class="akn-p">all parties that may be affected by the erection or display of such sign must be given opportunity for their input;</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_vii" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_vii"><span class="akn-num">(vii)</span><span class="akn-p">the municipality may require submission of impact assessment studies; and</span></span><span class="akn-item" id="att_17/para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_viii" data-eId="para_1__list_1__item_e__list_1__item_viii"><span class="akn-num">(viii)</span><span class="akn-p">no more than two individual signs of 6m × 3m each may be permitted, or alternatively one V-shaped sign with a maximum of two panels of 6m × 3m each on any one property. In addition, only one sign per street frontage will be permitted.</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>
</div>
<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_18" data-eId="att_18">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 18</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Tourism direction signs</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><section class="akn-section" id="att_18/sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Areas of control and consent</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_18/sec_1__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sign may be displayed in all areas of control.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_18/sec_1__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Display of a sign is subject to specific consent.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_18/sec_1__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sign may be displayed within a road reserve.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_18/sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Shape, size, height, colour, texture, layout of sign and dimensional detail of sign</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_18/sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_2__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of SADC-RTSM, Vol. 1, <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_4" href="#sec_4">Section 4</a>.10. Vol. 4, Chapter 7 applies.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_18/sec_3" data-eId="sec_3"><h3>3. Safety</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_18/sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_3__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The General engineering principles and guidelines in SADC-RTSM, with regard to traffic safety apply.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_18/sec_4" data-eId="sec_4"><h3>4. Design and construction</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_18/sec_4__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_4__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The general guidelines and conditions in SADC-RTSM with regard to the design and construction of a road sign apply.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_18/sec_5" data-eId="sec_5"><h3>5. Maintenance</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_18/sec_5__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The general guidelines in SADC-RTSM with regard to the maintenance of a road traffic sign apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-remark" data-status="editorial">[Schedule 18 inserted by section (5) of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment">Amendment By-law, 2013</a>]</span></span></span></span></section></span></span>
</div>
<div class="akn-attachment" id="att_19" data-eId="att_19">
<h2 class="akn-heading">Schedule 19 (<a class="akn-ref" data-href="#section-7" href="#section-7">Section 7</a>(mm))</h2>
<h2 class="akn-subheading">Class 4(e): On-site tourist attraction signs</h2>
<span class="akn-doc" data-name="schedule"><span class="akn-mainBody"><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_1" data-eId="sec_1"><h3>1. Areas of control and consent</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_1__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sign may be displayed in all areas of control.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_1__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_1__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Display of a sign is subject to specific consent.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_2" data-eId="sec_2"><h3>2. Shape, size, and height</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_2__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An identification sign may not exceed a maximum size of 1,5 square metres.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_2__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">An information panel may not exceed a maximum size of 3 square metres.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_2__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_2__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sign and panels may not exceed a maximum height of 2 metres.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_3" data-eId="sec_3"><h3>3. Position</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_3__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sign may be displayed at the actual attraction.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_3__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">All information must be aimed at a tourist on foot and not at motorised traffic.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_3__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_3__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A guidance sign may not be displayed.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_4" data-eId="sec_4"><h3>4. Colour and texture</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_4__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sign must consist of soft and subdued colours that will harmonise with the environment.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_4__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Corporate colours of a sponsor may not dominate a sign or information panel.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_4__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Sponsor information must harmonise with the rest of the information on the sign or panel in terms of colour.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_4__subsec_4" data-eId="sec_4__subsec_4"><span class="akn-num">(4)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">In the instance where bright corporate colours and logos form a strong contrast with the rest of the design, such colours may not be used and logos must be limited in size.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_5" data-eId="sec_5"><h3>5. Content of sign</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_19/sec_5__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_5__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Only a limited amount of informantion on sponsors is allowed.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_6" data-eId="sec_6"><h3>6. Illumination and animation</h3>
<section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_6__subsec_1" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_1"><span class="akn-num">(1)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">External illumination is allowed in all areas of maximum control.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_6__subsec_2" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_2"><span class="akn-num">(2)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">Internal and external illumination is allowed in urban areas of partial and minimum control.</span></span></section><section class="akn-subsection" id="att_19/sec_6__subsec_3" data-eId="sec_6__subsec_3"><span class="akn-num">(3)</span><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">A sign may not be animated.</span></span></section></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_7" data-eId="sec_7"><h3>7. Safety</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_19/sec_7__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_7__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions relating to the safety of a sign apply.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_8" data-eId="sec_8"><h3>8. Design and construction</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_19/sec_8__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_8__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_10A" href="#sec_10A">section 10A</a> relating to the design and construction of a sign apply.</span></span></span></section><section class="akn-section" id="att_19/sec_9" data-eId="sec_9"><h3>9. Maintenance</h3>
<span class="akn-hcontainer" id="att_19/sec_9__hcontainer_1" data-eId="sec_9__hcontainer_1" data-name="hcontainer"><span class="akn-content"><span class="akn-p">The provisions of <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_20" href="#sec_20">section 20</a> relating to the maintenance of a sign and <a class="akn-ref" data-href="#sec_10B" href="#sec_10B">section 10B</a> apply.</span><span class="akn-p"><span class="akn-remark" data-status="editorial">[Schedule 19 inserted by section (6) of the <a class="akn-ref" data-href="/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment" href="https://edit.laws.africa/resolver/resolve/akn/za-wc013/act/by-law/2013/advertising-and-signage-amendment">Amendment By-law, 2013</a>]</span></span></span></span></section></span></span>
</div></span></article></span>





</div>
